***madras.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:madras.html>madras</a> (68888)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language"><a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:matras.html>matras</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Matratze</i> (<a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:high.html>High</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">materazzo</i>).

***magie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:magie.html>magie</a> (1883)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:magie.html>magie</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:magie.html>magie</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">magīa</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek"><a href = vnd.unilang:ancient.html>Ancient</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:greek.html>Greek</a></a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μαγεία</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mageía</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***magus.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:magus.html>magus</a> (51341)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek"><a href = vnd.unilang:ancient.html>Ancient</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:greek.html>Greek</a></a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μάγος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mágos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:magician.html>magician</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">Μάγος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Mágos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Magian</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:an.html>an</a> indeterminate <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Iranian_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Iranian languages"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> Iranian</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:origin.html>origin</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:see.html>see</a> <span class="polytonic" lang="grc">Μάγος</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="tr Latn">Mágos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:for.html>for</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a>)
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2"><a href = vnd.unilang:adjective.html>Adjective</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:magus.html>magus</a></strong> (<i><a href = vnd.unilang:feminine.html>feminine</a></i> <b class="Latn" lang="la">maga</b>, <i>neuter</i> <b class="Latn" lang="la">magum</b>); <i><a href = vnd.unilang:first.html>first</a>/second-declension <a href = vnd.unilang:adjective.html>adjective</a></i>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:magic.html>magic</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:magical.html>magical</a></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:magus.html>magus</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Latn" lang="la">magī</b>); <i><a href = vnd.unilang:second.html>second</a> declension</i>
</p>
<ol><li>(<a href = vnd.unilang:common.html>common</a> usage) <a href = vnd.unilang:magician.html>magician</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> derogatorily <a href = vnd.unilang:sorcerer.html>sorcerer</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:trickster.html>trickster</a>, conjurer, <a href = vnd.unilang:charlatan.html>charlatan</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:wizard.html>wizard</a></li>
<li>(<a href = vnd.unilang:special.html>special</a> usage) <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> Zoroastrian <a href = vnd.unilang:priest.html>priest</a></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mailen.html>mailen</a> (27049)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:e-mail.html>e-mail</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> -en appended <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> e- dropped.

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:mailen.html>mailen</a></b>
</p>
